\doxysubsubsection*{Driver version}
Configures whether to check a parameter in a function.

Some MCG settings must be changed with conditions, for example:\+
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item MCGIRCLK settings, such as the source, divider, and the trim value should not change when MCGIRCLK is used as a system clock source.
\item MCG\+\_\+\+C7\+[OSCSEL]\+ should not be changed when the external reference clock is used as a system clock source. For example, in FBE/\+\+BLPE/\+\+PBE modes.
\item The users should only switch between the supported clock modes.
\end{DoxyEnumerate}

MCG functions check the parameter and MCG status before setting, if not allowed to change, the functions return error. The parameter checking increases code size, if code size is a critical requirement, change \+\#\+MCG\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+CHECK\+\_\+\+PARAM to 0 to disable parameter checking.

Configure whether driver controls clock

When set to 0, peripheral drivers will enable clock in initialize function and disable clock in de-\/initialize function. When set to 1, peripheral driver will not control the clock, application could control the clock out of the driver.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
All drivers share this feature switcher. If it is set to 1, application should handle clock enable and disable for all drivers. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\Hypertarget{group__clock_ga08ae02d80a8028784fb267a3e4860ad7}\index{Clock@{Clock}!mcg\_config\_t@{mcg\_config\_t}}
\index{mcg\_config\_t@{mcg\_config\_t}!Clock@{Clock}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mcg\_config\_t}{mcg\_config\_t}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__clock_ga08ae02d80a8028784fb267a3e4860ad7} 
typedef struct \doxymbox{\hyperlink{struct__mcg__config}{\+\_\+mcg\+\_\+config}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__clock_ga08ae02d80a8028784fb267a3e4860ad7}{mcg\+\_\+config\+\_\+t}}}



MCG mode change configuration structure. 

When porting to a new board, set the following members according to the board setting:\+
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item frdiv:\+ If the FLL uses the external reference clock, set this value to ensure that the external reference clock divided by frdiv is in the 31.\+25 k\+Hz to 39.\+0625 k\+Hz range.
\item The PLL reference clock divider PRDIV:\+ PLL reference clock frequency after PRDIV should be in the FSL\+\_\+\+FEATURE\+\_\+\+MCG\+\_\+\+PLL\+\_\+\+REF\+\_\+\+MIN to FSL\+\_\+\+FEATURE\+\_\+\+MCG\+\_\+\+PLL\+\_\+\+REF\+\_\+\+MAX range. 
\end{DoxyEnumerate}\Hypertarget{group__clock_ga5a46989b0f514536b1809c59a45d603f}\index{Clock@{Clock}!osc\_config\_t@{osc\_config\_t}}
\index{osc\_config\_t@{osc\_config\_t}!Clock@{Clock}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{osc\_config\_t}{osc\_config\_t}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__clock_ga5a46989b0f514536b1809c59a45d603f} 
typedef struct \doxymbox{\hyperlink{struct__osc__config}{\+\_\+osc\+\_\+config}} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__clock_ga5a46989b0f514536b1809c59a45d603f}{osc\+\_\+config\+\_\+t}}}



OSC Initialization Configuration Structure. 

Defines the configuration data structure to initialize the OSC. When porting to a new board, set the following members according to the board setting:\+
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item freq:\+ The external frequency.
\item work\+Mode:\+ The OSC module mode. 
\end{DoxyEnumerate}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CLOCK\_CalcPllDiv()}{CLOCK\_CalcPllDiv()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__clock_ga5d00aed41e6ca9b0c49e69afbdd2ee1b} 
uint32\+\_\+t CLOCK\+\_\+\+Calc\+Pll\+Div (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ref\+Freq}{, }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{desire\+Freq}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{prdiv}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{vdiv}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Calculates the PLL divider setting for a desired output frequency. 

This function calculates the correct reference clock divider ({\ttfamily PRDIV}) and VCO divider ({\ttfamily VDIV}) to generate a desired PLL output frequency. It returns the closest frequency match with the corresponding {\ttfamily PRDIV/\+\+VDIV} returned from parameters. If a desired frequency is not valid, this function returns 0.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ref\+Freq} & PLL reference clock frequency. \\
\hline
{\em desire\+Freq} & Desired PLL output frequency. \\
\hline
{\em prdiv} & PRDIV value to generate desired PLL frequency. \\
\hline
{\em vdiv} & VDIV value to generate desired PLL frequency. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Closest frequency match that the PLL was able generate.
\end{DoxyReturn}
brief Calculates the PLL divider setting for a desired output frequency.

This function calculates the correct reference clock divider ({\ttfamily PRDIV}) and VCO divider ({\ttfamily VDIV}) to generate a desired PLL output frequency. It returns the closest frequency match with the corresponding {\ttfamily PRDIV/\+\+VDIV} returned from parameters. If a desired frequency is not valid, this function returns 0.

param ref\+Freq PLL reference clock frequency. param desire\+Freq Desired PLL output frequency. param prdiv PRDIV value to generate desired PLL frequency. param vdiv VDIV value to generate desired PLL frequency. return Closest frequency match that the PLL was able generate.

\Hypertarget{group__clock_ga4e9576040785a78e76d58ee18bfd086d}\index{Clock@{Clock}!CLOCK\_EnablePll0@{CLOCK\_EnablePll0}}
\index{CLOCK\_EnablePll0@{CLOCK\_EnablePll0}!Clock@{Clock}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CLOCK\_EnablePll0()}{CLOCK\_EnablePll0()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__clock_ga4e9576040785a78e76d58ee18bfd086d} 
void CLOCK\+\_\+\+Enable\+Pll0 (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__clock_ga06c8c72409b5034724e0819642531531}{mcg\+\_\+pll\+\_\+config\+\_\+t}} const \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{config}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Enables the PLL0 in FLL mode. 

This function sets us the PLL0 in FLL mode and reconfigures the PLL0. Ensure that the PLL reference clock is enabled before calling this function and that the PLL0 is not used as a clock source. The function CLOCK\+\_\+\+Calc\+Pll\+Div gets the correct PLL divider values.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em config} & Pointer to the configuration structure.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
brief Enables the PLL0 in FLL mode.

This function sets us the PLL0 in FLL mode and reconfigures the PLL0. Ensure that the PLL reference clock is enabled before calling this function and that the PLL0 is not used as a clock source. The function CLOCK\+\_\+\+Calc\+Pll\+Div gets the correct PLL divider values.

param config Pointer to the configuration structure.

\Hypertarget{group__clock_ga2608ce13724a29d6de5c78779f042c05}\index{Clock@{Clock}!CLOCK\_ExternalModeToFbeModeQuick@{CLOCK\_ExternalModeToFbeModeQuick}}
\index{CLOCK\_ExternalModeToFbeModeQuick@{CLOCK\_ExternalModeToFbeModeQuick}!Clock@{Clock}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CLOCK\_ExternalModeToFbeModeQuick()}{CLOCK\_ExternalModeToFbeModeQuick()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__clock_ga2608ce13724a29d6de5c78779f042c05} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ksdk__common_gaaabdaf7ee58ca7269bd4bf24efcde092}{status\+\_\+t}} CLOCK\+\_\+\+External\+Mode\+To\+Fbe\+Mode\+Quick (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void}]{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Switches the MCG to FBE mode from the external mode. 

This function switches the MCG from external modes (PEE/\+\+PBE/\+\+BLPE/\+\+FEE) to the FBE mode quickly. The external clock is used as the system clock source and PLL is disabled. However, the FLL settings are not configured. This is a lite function with a small code size, which is useful during the mode switch. For example, to switch from PEE mode to FEI mode:\+


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__clock_ga2608ce13724a29d6de5c78779f042c05}{CLOCK\_ExternalModeToFbeModeQuick}}();}
\DoxyCodeLine{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__clock_gab822037c5956542631165b6d1d1f6095}{CLOCK\_SetFeiMode}}(...);}

\end{DoxyCode}



\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em \doxylink{group__ksdk__common_gga2de26871206ca53c1e0de28629a20f02a829bee76c6b02225d9c891ae8ef70881}{k\+Status\+\_\+\+Success}} & Switched successfully. \\
\hline
{\em \doxylink{group__clock_gga284f80e967d9fe1f44b35a8f95fb4de3a0041b9349a72d85ca329d9c7da4543af}{k\+Status\+\_\+\+MCG\+\_\+\+Mode\+Invalid}} & If the current mode is not an external mode, do not call this function.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}
brief Switches the MCG to FBE mode from the external mode.

This function switches the MCG from external modes (PEE/\+\+PBE/\+\+BLPE/\+\+FEE) to the FBE mode quickly. The external clock is used as the system clock source and PLL is disabled. However, the FLL settings are not configured. This is a lite function with a small code size, which is useful during the mode switch. For example, to switch from PEE mode to FEI mode:\+

code \doxylink{group__clock_ga2608ce13724a29d6de5c78779f042c05}{CLOCK\+\_\+\+External\+Mode\+To\+Fbe\+Mode\+Quick()}; CLOCK\+\_\+\+Set\+Fei\+Mode(...); endcode

retval k\+Status\+\_\+\+Success Switched successfully. retval k\+Status\+\_\+\+MCG\+\_\+\+Mode\+Invalid If the current mode is not an external mode, do not call this function.

uint32\+\_\+t CLOCK\+\_\+\+Get\+Fll\+Freq (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void}]{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets the MCG FLL clock (MCGFLLCLK) frequency. 

This function gets the MCG FLL clock frequency in Hz based on the current MCG register value. The FLL is enabled in FEI/\+\+FBI/\+\+FEE/\+\+FBE mode and disabled in low power state in other modes.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The frequency of MCGFLLCLK.
\end{DoxyReturn}
brief Gets the MCG FLL clock (MCGFLLCLK) frequency.

This function gets the MCG FLL clock frequency in Hz based on the current MCG register value. The FLL is enabled in FEI/\+\+FBI/\+\+FEE/\+\+FBE mode and disabled in low power state in other modes.

return The frequency of MCGFLLCLK.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__clock_gad60a82bdcf832b1e7aee25ef98c5d8eb} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ksdk__common_gaaabdaf7ee58ca7269bd4bf24efcde092}{status\+\_\+t}} CLOCK\+\_\+\+Internal\+Mode\+To\+Fbi\+Mode\+Quick (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void}]{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Switches the MCG to FBI mode from internal modes. 

This function switches the MCG from internal modes (PEI/\+\+PBI/\+\+BLPI/\+\+FEI) to the FBI mode quickly. The MCGIRCLK is used as the system clock source and PLL is disabled. However, FLL settings are not configured. This is a lite function with a small code size, which is useful during the mode switch. For example, to switch from PEI mode to FEE mode:\+


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__clock_gad60a82bdcf832b1e7aee25ef98c5d8eb}{CLOCK\_InternalModeToFbiModeQuick}}();}
\DoxyCodeLine{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__clock_gaf1c10796ccee24f273e8cc709e87cc66}{CLOCK\_SetFeeMode}}(...);}

\end{DoxyCode}

\hline
{\em \doxylink{group__clock_gga284f80e967d9fe1f44b35a8f95fb4de3a0041b9349a72d85ca329d9c7da4543af}{k\+Status\+\_\+\+MCG\+\_\+\+Mode\+Invalid}} & If the current mode is not an internal mode, do not call this function.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}
brief Switches the MCG to FBI mode from internal modes.

This function switches the MCG from internal modes (PEI/\+\+PBI/\+\+BLPI/\+\+FEI) to the FBI mode quickly. The MCGIRCLK is used as the system clock source and PLL is disabled. However, FLL settings are not configured. This is a lite function with a small code size, which is useful during the mode switch. For example, to switch from PEI mode to FEE mode:\+

code \doxylink{group__clock_gad60a82bdcf832b1e7aee25ef98c5d8eb}{CLOCK\+\_\+\+Internal\+Mode\+To\+Fbi\+Mode\+Quick()}; CLOCK\+\_\+\+Set\+Fee\+Mode(...); endcode

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__clock_gaee21d3843fbef183136690d8a5cd1c67} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ksdk__common_gaaabdaf7ee58ca7269bd4bf24efcde092}{status\+\_\+t}} CLOCK\+\_\+\+Set\+External\+Ref\+Clk\+Config (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__clock_gab6d0b226b0a262b3e48c6173e8e90210}{mcg\+\_\+oscsel\+\_\+t}}}]{oscsel}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Selects the MCG external reference clock. 

Selects the MCG external reference clock source, changes the MCG\+\_\+\+C7\+[OSCSEL]\+, and waits for the clock source to be stable. Because the external reference clock should not be changed in FEE/\+\+FBE/\+\+BLPE/\+\+PBE/\+\+PEE modes, do not call this function in these modes.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em oscsel} & MCG external reference clock source, MCG\+\_\+\+C7\+[OSCSEL]\+. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em \doxylink{group__clock_gga284f80e967d9fe1f44b35a8f95fb4de3ae6a6ceb6edc94718fbcbb5436596ce22}{k\+Status\+\_\+\+MCG\+\_\+\+Source\+Used}} & Because the external reference clock is used as a clock source, the configuration should not be changed. Otherwise, a glitch occurs. \\
\hline
{\em \doxylink{group__ksdk__common_gga2de26871206ca53c1e0de28629a20f02a829bee76c6b02225d9c891ae8ef70881}{k\+Status\+\_\+\+Success}} & External reference clock set successfully.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}
brief Selects the MCG external reference clock.

Selects the MCG external reference clock source, changes the MCG\+\_\+\+C7\+[OSCSEL]\+, and waits for the clock source to be stable. Because the external reference clock should not be changed in FEE/\+\+FBE/\+\+BLPE/\+\+PBE/\+\+PEE modes, do not call this function in these modes.

param oscsel MCG external reference clock source, MCG\+\_\+\+C7\+[OSCSEL]\+. retval k\+Status\+\_\+\+MCG\+\_\+\+Source\+Used Because the external reference clock is used as a clock source, the configuration should not be changed. Otherwise, a glitch occurs. retval k\+Status\+\_\+\+Success External reference clock set successfully.

\Hypertarget{group__clock_gad9ad302c9dd07e99396916073a4a5b65}\index{Clock@{Clock}!CLOCK\_SetInternalRefClkConfig@{CLOCK\_SetInternalRefClkConfig}}
\index{CLOCK\_SetInternalRefClkConfig@{CLOCK\_SetInternalRefClkConfig}!Clock@{Clock}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CLOCK\_SetInternalRefClkConfig()}{CLOCK\_SetInternalRefClkConfig()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__clock_gad9ad302c9dd07e99396916073a4a5b65} 
\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ksdk__common_gaaabdaf7ee58ca7269bd4bf24efcde092}{status\+\_\+t}} CLOCK\+\_\+\+Set\+Internal\+Ref\+Clk\+Config (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{enable\+Mode}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__clock_ga693d5d4ff2635ec4e14f5f0f528ac5b8}{mcg\+\_\+irc\+\_\+mode\+\_\+t}}}]{ircs}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{fcrdiv}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Configures the Internal Reference clock (MCGIRCLK). 

This function sets the {\ttfamily MCGIRCLK} base on parameters. It also selects the IRC source. If the fast IRC is used, this function sets the fast IRC divider. This function also sets whether the {\ttfamily MCGIRCLK} is enabled in stop mode. Calling this function in FBI/\+\+PBI/\+\+BLPI modes may change the system clock. As a result, using the function in these modes it is not allowed.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em enable\+Mode} & MCGIRCLK enable mode, OR\textquotesingle{}ed value of the enumeration \+\_\+mcg\+\_\+irclk\+\_\+enable\+\_\+mode. \\
\hline
{\em ircs} & MCGIRCLK clock source, choose fast or slow. \\
\hline
{\em fcrdiv} & Fast IRC divider setting ({\ttfamily FCRDIV}). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em \doxylink{group__clock_gga284f80e967d9fe1f44b35a8f95fb4de3ae6a6ceb6edc94718fbcbb5436596ce22}{k\+Status\+\_\+\+MCG\+\_\+\+Source\+Used}} & Because the internal reference clock is used as a clock source, the configuration should not be changed. Otherwise, a glitch occurs. \\
\hline
{\em \doxylink{group__ksdk__common_gga2de26871206ca53c1e0de28629a20f02a829bee76c6b02225d9c891ae8ef70881}{k\+Status\+\_\+\+Success}} & MCGIRCLK configuration finished successfully.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}
brief Configures the Internal Reference clock (MCGIRCLK).

This function sets the {\ttfamily MCGIRCLK} base on parameters. It also selects the IRC source. If the fast IRC is used, this function sets the fast IRC divider. This function also sets whether the {\ttfamily MCGIRCLK} is enabled in stop mode. Calling this function in FBI/\+\+PBI/\+\+BLPI modes may change the system clock. As a result, using the function in these modes it is not allowed.

param enable\+Mode MCGIRCLK enable mode, OR\textquotesingle{}ed value of ref \+\_\+mcg\+\_\+irclk\+\_\+enable\+\_\+mode. param ircs MCGIRCLK clock source, choose fast or slow. param fcrdiv Fast IRC divider setting ({\ttfamily FCRDIV}). retval k\+Status\+\_\+\+MCG\+\_\+\+Source\+Used Because the internal reference clock is used as a clock source, the configuration should not be changed. Otherwise, a glitch occurs. retval k\+Status\+\_\+\+Success MCGIRCLK configuration finished successfully. 

Definition at line \doxymbox{\hyperlink{fsl__clock_8c_source_l00872}{872}} of file \doxymbox{\hyperlink{fsl__clock_8c_source}{fsl\+\_\+clock.\+c}}.

\Hypertarget{group__clock_ga53df74476e923504d75c4ac878979492}\index{Clock@{Clock}!CLOCK\_SetLowPowerEnable@{CLOCK\_SetLowPowerEnable}}
\index{CLOCK\_SetLowPowerEnable@{CLOCK\_SetLowPowerEnable}!Clock@{Clock}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CLOCK\_SetLowPowerEnable()}{CLOCK\_SetLowPowerEnable()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__clock_ga53df74476e923504d75c4ac878979492} 
void CLOCK\+\_\+\+Set\+Low\+Power\+Enable (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{enable}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [static]}}



Enables or disables the MCG low power. 

Enabling the MCG low power disables the PLL and FLL in bypass modes. In other words, in FBE and PBE modes, enabling low power sets the MCG to BLPE mode. In FBI and PBI modes, enabling low power sets the MCG to BLPI mode. When disabling the MCG low power, the PLL or FLL are enabled based on MCG settings.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em enable} & True to enable MCG low power, false to disable MCG low power. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}


Definition at line \doxymbox{\hyperlink{fsl__clock_8h_source_l00916}{916}} of file \doxymbox{\hyperlink{fsl__clock_8h_source}{fsl\+\_\+clock.\+h}}.

\hline

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item The parameter {\ttfamily pllcs} selects the PLL. For platforms with only one PLL, the parameter pllcs is kept for interface compatibility.
\item The parameter {\ttfamily config} is the PLL configuration structure. On some platforms, it is possible to choose the external PLL directly, which renders the configuration structure not necessary. In this case, pass in NULL. For example:\+ CLOCK\+\_\+\+Set\+Pbe\+Mode(k\+MCG\+\_\+\+Oscsel\+Osc, k\+MCG\+\_\+\+Pll\+Clk\+Sel\+Ext\+Pll, NULL);
\end{DoxyEnumerate}
\end{DoxyNote}

note
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item The parameter {\ttfamily pllcs} selects the PLL. For platforms with only one PLL, the parameter pllcs is kept for interface compatibility.
\item The parameter {\ttfamily config} is the PLL configuration structure. On some platforms, it is possible to choose the external PLL directly, which renders the configuration structure not necessary. In this case, pass in NULL. For example:\+ CLOCK\+\_\+\+Set\+Pbe\+Mode(k\+MCG\+\_\+\+Oscsel\+Osc, k\+MCG\+\_\+\+Pll\+Clk\+Sel\+Ext\+Pll, NULL); 
\end{DoxyEnumerate}

\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ksdk__common_gaaabdaf7ee58ca7269bd4bf24efcde092}{status\+\_\+t}} CLOCK\+\_\+\+Set\+Pee\+Mode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void}]{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the MCG to PEE mode. 

This function sets the MCG to PEE mode.


\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em \doxylink{group__clock_gga284f80e967d9fe1f44b35a8f95fb4de3ad992385c89093ce4e1fc3630e3fb7659}{k\+Status\+\_\+\+MCG\+\_\+\+Mode\+Unreachable}} & Could not switch to the target mode. \\
\hline
{\em \doxylink{group__ksdk__common_gga2de26871206ca53c1e0de28629a20f02a829bee76c6b02225d9c891ae8ef70881}{k\+Status\+\_\+\+Success}} & Switched to the target mode successfully.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This function only changes the CLKS to use the PLL/\+\+FLL output. If the PRDIV/\+\+VDIV are different than in the PBE mode, set them up in PBE mode and wait. When the clock is stable, switch to PEE mode.
\end{DoxyNote}
brief Sets the MCG to PEE mode.

This function sets the MCG to PEE mode.

retval k\+Status\+\_\+\+MCG\+\_\+\+Mode\+Unreachable Could not switch to the target mode. retval k\+Status\+\_\+\+Success Switched to the target mode successfully.

note This function only changes the CLKS to use the PLL/\+\+FLL output. If the PRDIV/\+\+VDIV are different than in the PBE mode, set them up in PBE mode and wait. When the clock is stable, switch to PEE mode.

\Hypertarget{group__clock_ga66760c2d7d5cff9225e57a30c3da1eb2}\index{Clock@{Clock}!CLOCK\_SetSimSafeDivs@{CLOCK\_SetSimSafeDivs}}
\index{CLOCK\_SetSimSafeDivs@{CLOCK\_SetSimSafeDivs}!Clock@{Clock}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CLOCK\_SetSimSafeDivs()}{CLOCK\_SetSimSafeDivs()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__clock_ga66760c2d7d5cff9225e57a30c3da1eb2} 
void CLOCK\+\_\+\+Set\+Sim\+Safe\+Divs (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void}]{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [static]}}



Set the system clock dividers in SIM to safe value. 

The system level clocks (core clock, bus clock, flexbus clock and flash clock) must be in allowed ranges. During MCG clock mode switch, the MCG output clock changes then the system level clocks may be out of range. This function could be used before MCG mode change, to make sure system level clocks are in allowed range. 

Definition at line \doxymbox{\hyperlink{fsl__clock_8h_source_l00842}{842}} of file \doxymbox{\hyperlink{fsl__clock_8h_source}{fsl\+\_\+clock.\+h}}.

\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ksdk__common_gaaabdaf7ee58ca7269bd4bf24efcde092}{status\+\_\+t}} CLOCK\+\_\+\+Trim\+Internal\+Ref\+Clk (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{ext\+Freq}{, }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{desire\+Freq}{, }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{actual\+Freq}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__clock_gae7437ec05ccdc9cf47d7130e26cd2f41}{mcg\+\_\+atm\+\_\+select\+\_\+t}}}]{atms}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Auto trims the internal reference clock. 

This function trims the internal reference clock by using the external clock. If successful, it returns the k\+Status\+\_\+\+Success and the frequency after trimming is received in the parameter {\ttfamily actual\+Freq}. If an error occurs, the error code is returned.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ext\+Freq} & External clock frequency, which should be a bus clock. \\
\hline
{\em desire\+Freq} & Frequency to trim to. \\
\hline
{\em actual\+Freq} & Actual frequency after trimming. \\
\hline
{\em atms} & Trim fast or slow internal reference clock. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em \doxylink{group__ksdk__common_gga2de26871206ca53c1e0de28629a20f02a829bee76c6b02225d9c891ae8ef70881}{k\+Status\+\_\+\+Success}} & ATM success. \\
\hline
{\em \doxylink{group__clock_gga284f80e967d9fe1f44b35a8f95fb4de3ab3046b9a3ac26a54a308b360ae1d6b6d}{k\+Status\+\_\+\+MCG\+\_\+\+Atm\+Bus\+Clock\+Invalid}} & The bus clock is not in allowed range for the ATM. \\
\hline

\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}
brief Auto trims the internal reference clock.

This function trims the internal reference clock by using the external clock. If successful, it returns the k\+Status\+\_\+\+Success and the frequency after trimming is received in the parameter p actual\+Freq. If an error occurs, the error code is returned.

param ext\+Freq External clock frequency, which should be a bus clock. param desire\+Freq Frequency to trim to. param actual\+Freq Actual frequency after trimming. param atms Trim fast or slow internal reference clock. retval k\+Status\+\_\+\+Success ATM success. retval k\+Status\+\_\+\+MCG\+\_\+\+Atm\+Bus\+Clock\+Invalid The bus clock is not in allowed range for the ATM. retval k\+Status\+\_\+\+MCG\+\_\+\+Atm\+Desired\+Freq\+Invalid MCGIRCLK could not be trimmed to the desired frequency. retval k\+Status\+\_\+\+MCG\+\_\+\+Atm\+Irc\+Used Could not trim because MCGIRCLK is used as a bus clock source. retval k\+Status\+\_\+\+MCG\+\_\+\+Atm\+Hardware\+Fail Hardware fails while trimming.

\Hypertarget{group__clock_ga70a4a6ffb6c5a7a271aad89fe482bafc}\index{Clock@{Clock}!g\_xtal0Freq@{g\_xtal0Freq}}
\index{g\_xtal0Freq@{g\_xtal0Freq}!Clock@{Clock}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{g\_xtal0Freq}{g\_xtal0Freq}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__clock_ga70a4a6ffb6c5a7a271aad89fe482bafc} 
volatile uint32\+\_\+t g\+\_\+xtal0\+Freq\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



External XTAL0 (OSC0) clock frequency. 

The XTAL0/\+\+EXTAL0 (OSC0) clock frequency in Hz. When the clock is set up, use the function CLOCK\+\_\+\+Set\+Xtal0\+Freq to set the value in the clock driver. For example, if XTAL0 is 8 MHz:\+ 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{Set\ up\ the\ OSC0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__clock_ga7fd566b301526150b4e2be076006029f}{CLOCK\_InitOsc0}}(...);}
\DoxyCodeLine{Set\ the\ XTAL0\ value\ to\ the\ clock\ driver.}
\DoxyCodeLine{CLOCK\_SetXtal0Freq(80000000);}

\end{DoxyCode}


This is important for the multicore platforms where only one core needs to set up the OSC0 using the CLOCK\+\_\+\+Init\+Osc0. All other cores need to call the CLOCK\+\_\+\+Set\+Xtal0\+Freq to get a valid clock frequency. 

Definition at line \doxymbox{\hyperlink{fsl__clock_8c_source_l00104}{104}} of file \doxymbox{\hyperlink{fsl__clock_8c_source}{fsl\+\_\+clock.\+c}}.

\Hypertarget{group__clock_ga170d2fd7c6b439b72e0f73b4d73443af}\index{Clock@{Clock}!g\_xtal32Freq@{g\_xtal32Freq}}
\index{g\_xtal32Freq@{g\_xtal32Freq}!Clock@{Clock}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{g\_xtal32Freq}{g\_xtal32Freq}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__clock_ga170d2fd7c6b439b72e0f73b4d73443af} 
volatile uint32\+\_\+t g\+\_\+xtal32\+Freq\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



External XTAL32/\+\+EXTAL32/\+\+RTC\+\_\+\+CLKIN clock frequency. 

The XTAL32/\+\+EXTAL32/\+\+RTC\+\_\+\+CLKIN clock frequency in Hz. When the clock is set up, use the function CLOCK\+\_\+\+Set\+Xtal32\+Freq to set the value in the clock driver.

This is important for the multicore platforms where only one core needs to set up the clock. All other cores need to call the CLOCK\+\_\+\+Set\+Xtal32\+Freq to get a valid clock frequency. 

Definition at line \doxymbox{\hyperlink{fsl__clock_8c_source_l00106}{106}} of file \doxymbox{\hyperlink{fsl__clock_8c_source}{fsl\+\_\+clock.\+c}}.
